undergo dental surgery , tell your dentist that you are being treated with thalidomide and inform your doctor about your dental treatment . while being treated with thalidomide accord , you should maintain good oral hygiene ( including regular teeth brushing ) and receive routine dental check - ups . discuss with your doctor the precautions needed to avoid infecting other people . other
